# Text Elements
Суть алгоритма:

Позволяет найти длины кратчайших путей 
от какой-либо вершины до всех остальных вершин 
во взвешенном графе с неотрицательным весом рёбер. ^6YnW8V9b

A -> A = 0

2 ^1KJhHoXg

Из непосещённых вершин выбираем ту, у которой минимальное расстояние до A
и рассматриваем все её соседние непосещённые вершины.

Кратчайший путь из выбранной вершины X в соседнюю вершину Y будет равен:

min(dist(Y), dist(X) + weight(X, Y)), где:

dist(T) - текущее расстояние от A до T
weight(P, Q) - вес ребра из P в Q ^PdM8nut4

Вершина с минимальным расстоянием до A ^waCQJUYV

Полученные расстояния от A до остальных вершин графа:

A -> A = 0
A -> B = 1
A -> F = 2
A -> C = 4
A -> E = 5
A -> D = 9 ^ZEl7xon7

Код на Python:


import heapq


def naive_dijkstra(graph, start):
    distances = [float('inf')] * len(graph)
    distances[start] = 0

    visited = [False] * len(graph)

    for _ in range(len(graph)):
        min_distance = float('inf')
        min_index = -1

        for i in range(len(graph)):
            if not visited[i] and distances[i] < min_distance:
                min_distance = distances[i]
                min_index = i

        visited[min_index] = True

        for i in range(len(graph)):
            if graph[min_index][i] != 0 and not visited[i]:
                distances[i] = min(
                    distances[i], distances[min_index] + graph[min_index][i])

    return distances


def heap_dijkstra(graph, start):
    distances = [float('inf')] * len(graph)
    distances[start] = 0

    visited = [False] * len(graph)

    heap = [(0, start)]

    while heap:
        min_distance, min_index = heapq.heappop(heap)

        if visited[min_index]:
            continue

        visited[min_index] = True

        for i in range(len(graph)):
            if graph[min_index][i] != 0 and not visited[i]:
                distances[i] = min(
                    distances[i], distances[min_index] + graph[min_index][i])
                heapq.heappush(heap, (distances[i], i))

    return distances
 ^sEEHACtS

Код на C++:


#include <limits>
#include <queue>
#include <vector>

std::vector<int> naive_dijkstra(const std::vector<std::vector<int>> &graph, int start) {
    const int MAX_INT = std::numeric_limits<int>::max();
    int n = graph.size();
    std::vector<int> dist(n, MAX_INT);
    std::vector<bool> visited(n, false);
    dist[start] = 0;
    for (int i = 0; i < n; ++i) {
        int min_dist = MAX_INT;
        int min_idx = -1;
        for (int j = 0; j < n; ++j) {
            if (!visited[j] && dist[j] < min_dist) {
                min_dist = dist[j];
                min_idx = j;
            }
        }
        if (min_idx == -1) {
            break;
        }
        visited[min_idx] = true;
        for (int j = 0; j < n; ++j) {
            if (!visited[j] && graph[min_idx][j] != MAX_INT) {
                dist[j] = std::min(dist[j], dist[min_idx] + graph[min_idx][j]);
            }
        }
    }
    return dist;
}

std::vector<int> heap_dijkstra(const std::vector<std::vector<int>> &graph, int start) {
    const int MAX_INT = std::numeric_limits<int>::max();
    int n = graph.size();
    std::vector<int> dist(n, MAX_INT);
    std::vector<bool> visited(n, false);
    dist[start] = 0;
    std::priority_queue<std::pair<int, int>, std::vector<std::pair<int, int>>, std::greater<std::pair<int, int>>> pq;
    pq.push(std::make_pair(0, start));
    while (!pq.empty()) {
        int min_dist = pq.top().first;
        int min_idx = pq.top().second;
        pq.pop();
        if (visited[min_idx]) {
            continue;
        }
        visited[min_idx] = true;
        for (int j = 0; j < n; ++j) {
            if (!visited[j] && graph[min_idx][j] != MAX_INT) {
                dist[j] = std::min(dist[j], dist[min_idx] + graph[min_idx][j]);
                pq.push(std::make_pair(dist[j], j));
            }
        }
    }
    return dist;
}
 ^L70Ji31j

Сложность алгоритма:

Наивная реализация - O(EV)
Реализация с использованием кучи - O(E logV) ^L8CVuVKo

			"originalText": "Код на C++:\n\n\n#include <limits>\n#include <queue>\n#include <vector>\n\nstd::vector<int> naive_dijkstra(const std::vector<std::vector<int>> &graph, int start) {\n    const int MAX_INT = std::numeric_limits<int>::max();\n    int n = graph.size();\n    std::vector<int> dist(n, MAX_INT);\n    std::vector<bool> visited(n, false);\n    dist[start] = 0;\n    for (int i = 0; i < n; ++i) {\n        int min_dist = MAX_INT;\n        int min_idx = -1;\n        for (int j = 0; j < n; ++j) {\n            if (!visited[j] && dist[j] < min_dist) {\n                min_dist = dist[j];\n                min_idx = j;\n            }\n        }\n        if (min_idx == -1) {\n            break;\n        }\n        visited[min_idx] = true;\n        for (int j = 0; j < n; ++j) {\n            if (!visited[j] && graph[min_idx][j] != MAX_INT) {\n                dist[j] = std::min(dist[j], dist[min_idx] + graph[min_idx][j]);\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    return dist;\n}\n\nstd::vector<int> heap_dijkstra(const std::vector<std::vector<int>> &graph, int start) {\n    const int MAX_INT = std::numeric_limits<int>::max();\n    int n = graph.size();\n    std::vector<int> dist(n, MAX_INT);\n    std::vector<bool> visited(n, false);\n    dist[start] = 0;\n    std::priority_queue<std::pair<int, int>, std::vector<std::pair<int, int>>, std::greater<std::pair<int, int>>> pq;\n    pq.push(std::make_pair(0, start));\n    while (!pq.empty()) {\n        int min_dist = pq.top().first;\n        int min_idx = pq.top().second;\n        pq.pop();\n        if (visited[min_idx]) {\n            continue;\n        }\n        visited[min_idx] = true;\n        for (int j = 0; j < n; ++j) {\n            if (!visited[j] && graph[min_idx][j] != MAX_INT) {\n                dist[j] = std::min(dist[j], dist[min_idx] + graph[min_idx][j]);\n                pq.push(std::make_pair(dist[j], j));\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    return dist;\n}\n",
